<div id="review_561476153" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/561476153" />
    <a title="AJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3143126-aj"><img alt="AJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406382884p2/3143126.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/561476153?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AJ" href="/user/show/3143126-aj">AJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8153424-ecstasy-unveiled">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=romantic">romantic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=actiony">actiony</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3143126-aj?shelf=pb-i-own">pb-i-own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer561476153" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11346855889887036151">And the awesome continues!<br/><br/>Book 4 in the Demonica series brings us the story of Lore… the newly discovered brother of Eidolon, Shade and Wraith. An enslaved assassin, he is brought screeching into his brother’s lives when his next target hits very close to their hearts. To complicate matters, Lore’s target has an angel protecting them – Idess, a sexy, sassy female who knows how to kick some ass. <br/><br/>I absolutely adore Lore! Tortured, cynical, and seemingly indifferent to all that goes on around him, </span>
  <span id="freeText11346855889887036151" style="display:none">And the awesome continues!<br /><br />Book 4 in the Demonica series brings us the story of Lore… the newly discovered brother of Eidolon, Shade and Wraith. An enslaved assassin, he is brought screeching into his brother’s lives when his next target hits very close to their hearts. To complicate matters, Lore’s target has an angel protecting them – Idess, a sexy, sassy female who knows how to kick some ass. <br /><br />I absolutely adore Lore! Tortured, cynical, and seemingly indifferent to all that goes on around him, his supernatural gift is a ‘death touch’ that has kept him forcibly isolated for most of his life. But he has a deeply caring side that we see early on, and which is ramped up hugely when Idess comes along and totally rocks his world. Idess is a great heroine! She’s tough and single-minded, but is also dealing with her own issues from the past. Lore and Idess are both, for their own (very personal) reasons, committed to their tasks. So when they collide… fireworks! <br /><br />With brilliant fight scenes, wicked banter, and scorching chemistry, Lore and Idess have a sensational relationship that grows from sworn enemies to reluctant allies to friends and eventually lovers. And with the added complication of Lore being a Seminus demon, and needing sex in order to survive, it’s a wild ride!<br /><br />In addition to the brewing romance, there is a deep look into the disturbing and gory world of demon assassins, two of the most evil of evil bad guys on the prowl, family secrets uncovered, and major trouble brewing for one particular supernatural group. Yep, there’s a lot going on in this book, and I loved watching all of the different threads come together. I didn’t see the big twist coming, and had a massive ‘OMG’ moment, as well as lots of scares and squees as the story shifted all over the place. <br /><br />The group of key characters in this series continues to grow, but I love that Ione continues to keep the characters that we love from the previous books as a main part of the action. In fact, I think one of the best thing about these books is the dynamic between the characters. Between siblings, couples, friends and enemies, there is fighting, teasing, playfulness and brilliant banter, as well as deep, familial love and respect, gorgeous swoony moments and a whole lot of hotness. It’s all just epic!<br /><br />The next book is set up very nicely as we get to spend a lot of time with the heroine of book 5, Sin, and the spark of her love story has been lit with a hot moment between her and her love interest (love him!). There is some awesome chemistry there, as well as some pretty massive hurdles for the couple to overcome. I can’t wait to see where the story goes!<br /><br />If you haven’t read any of these books yet, GET INTO IT! Larissa Ione has created a unique paranormal world filled with brilliant characters, awesome supernatural powers and intriguing politics. These books are dark and dirty, but also hilarious, with lots of romance, sex and action, and a fantastic world that becomes more evolved with each book. I’m absolutely loving it.<br /><br />5 PNR-loving stars. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11346855889887036151" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_93116170" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/93116170" />
    <a title="Catherine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3282244-catherine"><img alt="Catherine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1277923282p2/3282244.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/93116170?book_show_action=true">Mar 08, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catherine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catherine" href="/user/show/3282244-catherine">Catherine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=fantasy-paranormal-sci-fi">fantasy-paranormal-sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3282244-catherine?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer93116170" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6890962482595705328">I was browsing the bookstore when this cover caught my eye. I read the back of it and figured I'd give it a try. I wish I would have known it was part of a series first. Unfortunately this book does not stand on its own well at all. There were so many characters running around that I was irritated. I found Lore's newly discovered brothers especially irritating. I suppose if I had read their books first I would have had some investment in them and might have been glad to read about them again. Ob</span>
  <span id="freeText6890962482595705328" style="display:none">I was browsing the bookstore when this cover caught my eye. I read the back of it and figured I'd give it a try. I wish I would have known it was part of a series first. Unfortunately this book does not stand on its own well at all. There were so many characters running around that I was irritated. I found Lore's newly discovered brothers especially irritating. I suppose if I had read their books first I would have had some investment in them and might have been glad to read about them again. Obviously that wasn't the case with me.<br /><br />Lore can kill with a touch (even inadvertently) which makes it very awkward for him to have the sex that he needs to keep his rage down. He's also bound to Deth as an assassin until he completes his 100th kill. His last kill is assigned to him and this time he isn't given the option to say no. Deth also gives him a time limit that he has to complete his last kill by or his sister, Sin, will die. Needless to say he's determined to kill the guy even though it will put him at odds with his brothers.<br /><br />While trying to take out his target he comes into contact with Idess. She's basically an angel-in-waiting and guards people who have an important destiny until she finally makes it to heaven. One of the people that Idess is assigned to guard is the very same person that Lore has to kill. Idess and Lore have several confrontations until Idess gets the upper hand. Unfortunately for Idess another one of the people she has to protect is in danger too. She ends up very busy trying to keep all of her charges safe.<br /><br />Idess and Lore seem to have good chemistry together. There's nice sexual tension between them and their dialogue together is amusing. I think if more time had been spent on developing them and their relationship I would have been happier. I could never forget that they had known each other a matter of days when they were overcome with love. There was way too much page time devoted to other characters and it definitely impacted the believability of the main character's romance for me.<br /><br />The type of book this was and tone of it really reminded me of Kresley Cole's Immortals After Dark series. I think if you enjoy those books you might like these ones too. I'd definitely recommend starting with the first one though.<br /><br />I don't think I'll read any more in this series. I'm mildly interested in Sin's story but I think I would be just as lost to all the previous book references in that one as I was in this one. It really pulls you out of the story when you're constantly wondering what everyone is talking about.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6890962482595705328" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10404779359668167773"> **4 ½ stars**<br/><br/> Wow! This book is over the top! There is so much going on in this book you may think it will overwhelm you (if it does, slow down).I didn’t have a problem with it,I thought it is brilliant!! I have to hand it to Larissa it’s not one bit confusing. <br/> <br/> Now let me tell you what you’ll find in this book, assassins, ghost’s, a new sister to a few bro’s, action, great romance, angels, Grim reaper (I loved that one!), Evil villain (I never expected who it was, it floored me when I read it</span>
  <span id="freeText10404779359668167773" style="display:none"> **4 ½ stars**<br /><br /> Wow! This book is over the top! There is so much going on in this book you may think it will overwhelm you (if it does, slow down).I didn’t have a problem with it,I thought it is brilliant!! I have to hand it to Larissa it’s not one bit confusing. <br /> <br /> Now let me tell you what you’ll find in this book, assassins, ghost’s, a new sister to a few bro’s, action, great romance, angels, Grim reaper (I loved that one!), Evil villain (I never expected who it was, it floored me when I read it). And there is some humor and of course those gorgeous demon’s, their wives and babies. Also, this book can be sad at times so add plenty emotions too.<br /><br /> The only reason why I did not give 5 stars is, it has so much going on I didn’t get the feel of Lore and Idess as much as I would have liked to.<br /><br /> I really hate to give out any spoilers for this book because it just is an excellent book, but for those who have to have it, please continue.<br /> <br />** some spoilers below**<br /><br /> Idess is a Memitim angel that has to protect Kynan. Lore is an assassin that has been charged to kill Kynan by his master and tries to do just that until he end’s up chained to a bed by Idess. Idess finds that Lore is one of her Promori and can’t kill him. But she has to keep Lore from killing Kynan to get her wings, so the only way was is to chain him to a bed. Will she have her way with Lore or not? It may surprise you. Now you will have to read for yourself to see how it turns out.<br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EYmic2c6+zovC755ZCR4ur+XNGWD1g310sJLYSEV1aMPOU+S33xnLgklGHu5qyPgW3ZYuONtH5Y5HsSGHz1Itw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('K5IyL9vvB5htste1k4qIE4HzDBh+nNeQfkBUr2KoJlI1It/OY6mbjEuccbdOBdNJZRJgxR4nxfOVnNtIXIC7Rg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer9958229829467392179">Air Force veteran Larissa Ione traded in a career in meteorology to pursue her passion of writing. She has since published dozens of books, hit several bestseller lists, including the New York Times and USA Today, and has been nominated for a RITA award. She now spends her days in pajamas with her computer, strong coffee, and supernatural worlds. She believes in celebrating everything, and would n</span>
  <span id="freeText9958229829467392179" style="display:none">Air Force veteran Larissa Ione traded in a career in meteorology to pursue her passion of writing. She has since published dozens of books, hit several bestseller lists, including the New York Times and USA Today, and has been nominated for a RITA award. She now spends her days in pajamas with her computer, strong coffee, and supernatural worlds. She believes in celebrating everything, and would never be caught without a bottle of Champagne chilling in the fridge…just in case. She currently lives in Wisconsin with her retired U.S. Coast Guard husband, her son, a rescue cat named Vegas, and her very own hellhounds, a King Shepherd named Hexe and a Belgian Malinois named Duvel.</span>

Smurfette is way hotter."<br />"What the fuck is a Smurfette?" Eidolon was seriously getting annoyed now.<br />"There's this cartoon called The Smurfs," Tayla explained, slowly, as though Eidolon were the child here.<br />"They're these little blue people, and they're all male. But one day a female shows up. She shouldn't exist, but she does."<br />Eidolon considered that for a second. "How did she get there?"<br />"An evil wizard named Gargamel made her," Tayla said. "In a lab or something."<br />"So you're suggesting that an evil wizard made Sin?"<br />"Of course not, silly. I'm just saying she's a Smurfette. A lone female amongst males."<br />Eidolon frowned. "Did the Smurfette mate with the males?"<br />"Dude." Wraith grimaced. "It's a cartoon.&rdquo;</span>
